class="details-section-contents show-more-container" jscontroller="G7YeLc" jsaction="rcuQ6b:rcuQ6b" data-show-use-buffer="true"> <div jscontroller="NlxvWb">  <h1 class="heading" tabindex="0"> Description </h1> <div class="show-more-content text-body" itemprop="description" tabindex="0"> <div jsname="C4s9Ed">Japanese is a Japanese-English offline dictionary featuring over 160000 entries, over 10000 kanji and almost 60000 example sentences.<p>Features<br>- Extremely fast search allows you to view results as you type.<br>- Results are ordered by reverence, with the best matches up the top<br>- Search using english, romaji, kanji or kana<br>- Advanced search features such as wildcards and logical AND (&amp; for many characters, ? for single characters, &amp; for AND)<br>- Includes handwriting recognition and component lookup to easily input kanji<br>- Entering in conjugated verbs will match the dictionary form ( -&gt; )<br>- Filter words by categories such as part of speech, field, terminology, JLPT or dialect<br>- Includes audio pronunciation for many words (requires internet connection)<br>- Example sentences include reading and links word entries<br>- Verb conjugation charts show how to conjugate verbs<br>- Includes common compounds for words and kanji<br>- Add notes to entries to leave yourself reminders<br>- Tag words to create lists which can be exported to csv or anki format<br>- History of items you have recently searched<br>- Includes animated stroke order diagrams to see how to write kanji<br>- Includes kana table</p></div>  <div class="show-more-end" Android!</span> Finally - a worthy Japanese dictionary, and a solid contender to similar apps available only on the iPhone. This app should definitely get more exposure! I could think of only two things that should be added: 1. Transitive and intransitive verbs should be linked to one another. Kana table should have animations, to show how each kana should be written. <div class="paragraph-end details-light"></div> </div> </div> </div> </div>  <div class="featured-review" data-expand-to="user-1" data-reviewid="gp:AOqpTOEJaBseyoYv6fPkYj1bDExo0E6gdOwSqpIpP3-8TeLIOP0bLOBmjgYnwQJu0jtoW-HIAa8V1d5yZV9VCQs" data-should-focus-specific-review="true" tabindex="0"> <div class="author">   <span> <span class="responsive-img-ldpi"> <span class="responsive-img author-image" style="background-image:url(https://lh4.ggpht.com/-wlenRvczHsA/AAAAAAAAAAI/AAAAAAAAAAA/p1A72HkNoV4/w48-c-h48/photo.jpg)"></span> </span> <span class="responsive-img-hdpi"> <span class="responsive-img author-image" style="background-image:url(https://lh4.ggpht.com/-wlenRvczHsA/AAAAAAAAAAI/AAAAAAAAAAA/p1A72HkNoV4/w96-c-h96/photo.jpg)"></span> </span> </span>  </div> <div> <span class="author-name">  Bob Dobbs </span> <div class="featured-review-star-rating">  <div class="tiny-star star-rating-non-editable-container" aria-label=" Rated 2 stars out of five stars "> <div class="current-rating" jsname="jIIjq" style="width: 40%;"></div> </div>  </div> <div class="quoted-review"> <div class="review-text"> <span class="review-title">It's OK, but not even close to the best</span> This used to be the best Japanese-English dictionary available for Android, but it's rarely updated (last update 2 YEARS AGO!). So while it has a nice layout, it hasn't kept up as competing apps quickly &amp; continuously improve. AEDICT3, for example, offers everything this app has, plus multiple dictionaries, a flexible attractive GUI, multiple input options, a myriad of import/export methods, add-on functions, and consistent updates from a responsive developer. This app seems ultra-generic by comparison! <div class="paragraph-end details-light"></div> </div> </div> </div> </div>  <div class="featured-review" data-expand-to="user-2" data-reviewid="gp:AOqpTOE2tHWFbKFu-LPACkJng3XNC-AzEBT1tnA-SeU8nYi-YU2l8CHWIo6UwjVCihtyA3wYezZD2-FfdBEbi9M" data-should-focus-specific-review="true" tabindex="0"> <div class="author">   <span> <span class="responsive-img-ldpi"> <span class="responsive-img author-image" style="background-image:url(https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-RQpUHD7MWzc/AAAAAAAAAAI/AAAAAAAAALM/kOUaYTS2ZUU/w48-c-h48/photo.jpg)"></span> </span> <span class="responsive-img-hdpi"> <span class="responsive-img author-image" style="background-image:url(https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-RQpUHD7MWzc/AAAAAAAAAAI/AAAAAAAAALM/kOUaYTS2ZUU/w96-c-h96/photo.jpg)"></span> </span> </span>  </div> <div> <span class="author-name">  Medieval Exponents </span> <div class="featured-review-star-rating">  <div class="tiny-star star-rating-non-editable-container" aria-label=" Rated 4 stars out of five stars "> <div class="current-rating" jsname="jIIjq" style="width: 80%;"></div> </div>  </div> <div class="quoted-review"> <div class="review-text"> <span class="review-title">Needs just a little more</span> It's a great dictionary for Kanji, but it'd be infinitely better if I could write out Hiragana and Katakana in the handwriting area. At least I can easily get results typing Romanji but it doesn't make for good immersion practice. <div class="paragraph-end details-light"></div> </div> </div> </div> </div>  <div class="featured-review" data-expand-to="user-3" data-reviewid="gp:AOqpTOE6io1OpNogiS8_GMkokMkS0HgyL6aXIIhx3G6-tzL8XoLQAbe_VJdQmKU1tuuN7kXfCzkrBPNJxkmArV0" data-should-focus-specific-review="true" tabindex="0"> <div class="author">   <span> <span class="responsive-img-ldpi"> <span class="responsive-img author-image" style="background-image:url(https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-o9D5Ln_8orc/AAAAAAAAAAI/AAAAAAAAAIE/1H00XumMMZ4/w48-c-h48/photo.jpg)"></span> </span> <span class="responsive-img-hdpi"> <span class="responsive-img author-image" style="background-image:url(https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-o9D5Ln_8orc/AAAAAAAAAAI/AAAAAAAAAIE/1H00XumMMZ4/w96-c-h96/photo.jpg)"></span> </span> </span>  </div> <div> <span class="author-name">  Alicorn Grandmaster </span> <div class="featured-review-star-rating">  <div class="tiny-star star-rating-non-editable-container" aria-label=" Rated 5 stars out of five stars "> <div class="current-rating" jsname="jIIjq" style="width: 100%;"></div> </div>  </div> <div class="quoted-review"> <div class="review-text"> <span class="review-title">Absolutely Brilliant and Simple!</span> This application is very useful for me with utilising the Kanji characters accurately, but I find the audio a bit annoying to deal with. Naturally, I listen to the sound a few times, then use some Roumaji translator to decypher what it sounds like. If I would recommend one improvement to this software, I would recommend adding a Roumaji and Hiragana text translation option and a "syllable-to-syllable" audio function. Also, this application needs some "common phrase" translations. Please fix the kanji recognition and I will rate a 5 <div class="review-link" style="display:none"> <a class="id-no-nav play-button tiny" href="#" target="_blank"> Full Review </a> </div> </div>
